      :ARG1 (x / گفتن
            :ARG0 (x2 / کس
                  :mod (x3 / چنین))
            :ARG1 (b / be-located-at-91
                  :ARG1 (x4 / گل
                        :poss x2)

                        :ARG1-of (i2 / include-01

            :ARG2 x2)

                  :mod (x11 / یکدفعه)
                  :condition (x12 / خوردن
                        :ARG0 (x13 / گوسفند)
                        :ARG1 x4))
            :beneficiary x2))
